-- Table structure for table `activity_assignee`

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `activity_assignee`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `activity_assignee` (
  `Activity_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Person_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Role_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Last_active_date` date NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00',
  UNIQUE KEY `Activity_id` (`Activity_id`,`Person_id`,`Role_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--
-- Table structure for table `personrole`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `personrole`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `personrole` (
  `Role_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Name` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `Level` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`Role_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=19 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `praanta`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `praanta`;
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `praanta` (
  `Praanta_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Name` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `Description` varchar(70) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `Praanta_type_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Coordinator_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Parent_praanta_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `Geo_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `URL` varchar(70) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Praanta_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `Name` (`Name`,`Parent_praanta_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=232 ;
